**Actions taken**:
1. Called `blofin_get_ticker` for TAC‑USDT (twice, same result).  
2. Received ticker snapshot:

   - 24h high 0.065626, low 0.039996, open 0.062772.

**Key insights**:
- Sharp 34 % drop from open to current price; price near 24h low.  
- Wide 24h range (high‑low swing ≈ 62 %) indicates high volatility and potential for large moves.  
- Liquidity is adequate (high volume) though depth beyond top level needs verification.  
- Current price near low suggests upside potential toward the 24h high (>50 % gain) if reversal occurs; downside limited as price already near floor.

**Open questions / next steps**:
- Obtain order‑book depth (`blofin_get_order_book`) to confirm deeper liquidity.  
- Fetch funding rate (`blofin_get_funding_rate`) for TAC‑USDT to assess long/short bias.  
- Run technical analysis (`blofin_technical_analysis`) for EMA, RSI, support/resistance, trend scores.  
- After gathering those data, compute suggested_side (likely long if reversal bias), estimate move_potential_pct, assign confidence, decide any veto, and craft thesis for JSON output.
